<a id="main-content"></a>
<div class="hidden" data-drupal-messages-fallback=""></div> <div about="/legal/privacy-notice" class="page full clearfix" role="article" typeof="schema:WebPage">
<span class="hidden" content="Privacy Policy" property="schema:name"></span>
<div class="content">
<div class="paragraph paragraph--naming-layer paragraph--o-a1 o-a1--default pad-top-lg pad-bottom-lg normal-color" id="" style="display: none;">
<div class="paragraph--container-layer">
<div class="container-fluid wrap">
<div class="row">
<div class="col-xs paragraph-content-section">
<div class="paragraph--m-text text-align-left">
<style>
.sketchup-privacy-policy {
    padding: 30px 0;
}

.page-header {
    display: none;
}

.page-section {
    padding: 30px 0px;
}

.page-section:first-child {
    padding: 0 0 30px 0;
}

hr {
    margin: 0;
}
</style>
<div class="sketchup-privacy-policy">
<div class="page-section">
<h1>
            SketchUp, Trimble, and Your Privacy
        </h1>
<p>
            As part of Trimble, we are dedicated to keeping your data private and
            secure. We are also committed to transparency, so we want you to understand
            the information we may collect from you and why we collect it. The
            following is a supplement to <a href="http://www.trimble.com/privacy.aspx">Trimble’s privacy commitment</a>.
        </p>
<p>
            The information we collect falls into three categories:
        </p>
<br/>
<div class="row f-flex">
<div class="col-xs-12 col-lg-4 margin-bottom-lg margin-bottom-lg-none">
<div class="ter-card height-100">
<div class="ter-card__body">
<p>
<b>Purchase Information</b>
</p>
<p>
                            When you purchase or use one of our free products, we collect basic
                            information provided by you to ensure a record of your purchase and
                            entitlements.
                        </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="col-xs-12 col-lg-4 margin-bottom-lg margin-bottom-lg-none">
<div class="ter-card height-100">
<div class="ter-card__body">
<p>
<b>Usage Information</b>
</p>
<p>
                            We capture information that helps us understand your experience with SketchUp, so that we can offer you more helpful content to help you get better at the software you're working with. We do use some of this information to serve you applicable content through digital advertising, email, and web properties.
                        </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="col-xs-12 col-lg-4 margin-bottom-lg margin-bottom-lg-none">
<div class="ter-card height-100">
<div class="ter-card__body">
<p>
<b>Profile Information</b>
</p>
<p>
                            We store information you provide to us to maintain a profile associated
                            with your Trimble account. We use this information to communicate with you,
                            and we never share it with third parties unless you explicitly ask us to, helpful content to help you get better at the software you're working with, and you will always have the ability to update, remove, or add information as desired.
                        </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<br/><br/>
<p>
            You can always manage your <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com/">SketchUp privacy preferences</a>, and below you’ll find a more detailed look at how our products and services utilize your data.
        </p>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp Pro
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            SketchUp Pro validates the software license at the time of installation,
            and collects activation details when the product starts up. The activation
            details provide anonymized information regarding the environment the
            application is running in. Specifically, we capture the following:
        </p>
<ul>
<li>
                Globally unique user ID - Completely anonymous
            </li>
<li>
                License state - Trial vs Purchased
            </li>
<li>
                Basic product information such as version, operating environment,
                language, and OpenGL version
            </li>
</ul>
<p>
            Network versions of SketchUp Pro also collect information to make sure
            that the software is used in compliance with the number of licenses
            purchased. If, for example, a user purchased a network license with 200
            seats, we will count how many seats are currently being used and will allow
            200 clients to runs concurrently.
        </p>
<p>
            SketchUp Pro uses third-party software to collect error and crash
            information. The collection and submission of data is voluntary and you
            will be asked whether or not you would like to submit the information at
            the time of the crash.
        </p>
<p>
            SketchUp Pro relies on Trimble ID for authentication and does not store any
            user information within the product. Trimble ID collects your first and last name, and email address. This information is required to utilize any products
            which require authentication (sign in).
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            The metrics are anonymous and we use the data to validate software use and
            prevent piracy. We also use them to understand product usage and to improve
            the product’s performance.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You can access your license information from the SketchUp menu bar. Updates
            to licenses must be made through the
            <a href="https://help.sketchup.com/en/contact/customer-support">
                help of a customer service representative
            </a>
            in order to protect the validity of the license. You may also review your license through our <a href="https://www.sketchup.com/license/renew">license manager</a>.
        </p>
<p>
            You can find supplemental product specific terms in the <a href="https://www.sketchup.com/license/f/sketchup">SketchUp Pro end user license agreement</a>.
        </p>
<h4>
            SketchUp Pro and V-Ray integration
        </h4>
<p>
V-Ray<sup>®</sup> is a plug-in developed by <a href="https://www.chaosgroup.com/">Chaos<sup>®</sup> Group</a> and used to render photorealistic visualizations.  The plug-in is bundled with the SketchUp Studio subscription offering exclusively. SketchUp will share personally identifiable information with Chaos Group if you choose to use the V-Ray extension. The use of the V-Ray plugin conforms to <a href="https://www.chaosgroup.com/privacy">Chaos Group’s privacy policy</a>. 
</p>
<p class="font-size-sm">Chaos<sup>®</sup> and V-Ray<sup>®</sup> are registered trademarks of Chaos Software OOD in Bulgaria and/or other countries.</p>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp Free
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            SketchUp Free relies on Trimble ID for authentication and does not store any user information within the product. Trimble ID collects your first and last name, and email address. This information is required to utilize any products which require authentication (sign in). SketchUp Free also relies on Trimble Connect for project management and file storage. Learn more about <a href="http://connect.trimble.com/">Trimble Connect.</a> Please see the <a href="https://community.trimble.com/docs/DOC-10003-terms-of-service"> Trimble Connect terms of service </a> for more information.</p>
<p>
            SketchUp Free collects usage information, such as user activity,
            performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses,
            browser type, and error and crash information.
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            SketchUp Free uses the Trimble ID service to validate the use of our free
            product and to link you to your Trimble Connect account. The metrics are
            anonymous and we use them to understand product usage and to improve the
            product’s performance.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You can access your account information by logging onto the SketchUp Free application and clicking on the preferences button in the top left hand corner of the page. To delete your account, please use the <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com">delete your data form</a>.
        </p>
<p>
            You can find supplemental product specific terms in the <a href="https://app.sketchup.com/tos.html">SketchUp Free Terms of Service</a>.
        </p>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp for Schools
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>SketchUp for Schools integrates with Google’s G Suite for EDU and Microsoft Education. Students log in through their Google or Microsoft account, and SketchUp does not receive any student information. Server logs collect information about requests made to the server, and include IP addresses, but do not collect user-specific information. SketchUp for Schools does not collect any registration data or account data for any of its users. Rather, this information is submitted directly to Google and Microsoft's services and is never stored by us. For additional information, please visit the <a href="https://app.sketchup.com/tos.html">SketchUp for Schools terms of service</a>.</p>
<p>SketchUp for Schools collects usage information, such as user activity, performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses, browser type, and error and crash information. All information is anonymized and cannot be tracked back to an individual.</p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            The metrics are anonymous and we use them to understand product usage and
            to improve the product’s performance.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>SketchUp for Schools does not collect any user data. Requests for access to user data need to be submitted to <a href="https://edu.google.com/k-12-solutions/g-suite">Google's G Suite for EDU</a> or to <a href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/education">Microsoft Education</a>.</p>
<p>You can find supplemental product specific terms in the <a href="https://app.sketchup.com/tos.html">SketchUp for Schools Terms of Service</a>.</p>

</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp Viewer
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            In order to download SketchUp models on mobile devices, headsets, and other
            compatible hardware, SketchUp Viewer allows users to sign in to 3D
            Warehouse, Trimble Connect, Dropbox, the iOS Files App, and/or other
            applications. SketchUp Viewer does not store any personal information
            within the product.
        </p>
<p>
            SketchUp Viewer collects usage information, such as user activity,
            performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses,
            device IDs, device type, error and crash information.
        </p>
<h4>ARCore</h4>
<p>ARCore is Android's SDK for Augmented Reality which allows you to view your models in AR in SketchUp Viewer. For further information about ARCore privacy practices, please read its <a href="http://www.google.com/policies/privacy/partners/">privacy policy</a></p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            The metrics are anonymous and we use them to understand product usage and
            to improve the product’s performance.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You have direct control over which cloud services SketchUp Viewer has
            access to, to sign out from a cloud service go to the Main Menu &gt;
            Accounts from within the application. To delete a model from the
            application, on the Home Screen, select the Information icon &gt; Delete on
            the model you wish to delete.
        </p>
<br/>
<p>
            Here's how to find supplemental product specific terms:
        </p>
<ul>
<li>
                HoloLens: within the application, go to Main Menu &gt; Legal &gt; EULA
            </li>
<li>
                iOS and Android: within the application, go to Main Menu &gt; Legal
                &gt; EULA -or- <a href="https://www.sketchup.com/license/b/sketchup-mobile-viewer">view the terms online</a>.
            </li>
</ul>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            3D Warehouse
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
<a href="https://3dwarehouse.sketchup.com">3D Warehouse</a>
            allows you to upload, download, and view 3D models. You can keep models
            private or share them with the 3D Warehouse user community. 3D Warehouse
            stores the models for you, allows you to comment on models of others and to
            manage access to your models. 3D Warehouse relies on Trimble ID for
            authentication. A 3D Warehouse profile is created for you when you log in
            with Google or Trimble ID for the first time. You can choose to add
            information about yourself or not. This information can include an avatar,
            first name, last name, websites you own, and social media accounts. You
            have the ability to opt in to notifications through your profile. Your
            profile information is stored within a 3D Warehouse database and is never
            shared with third parties.
        </p>
<p>
            You have the ability to upload your models and make them available for
            download by the 3D Warehouse community, or keep them private and not
            accessible by the community. Models shared on 3D Warehouse can be
            downloaded and saved by community members onto their personal computers or
            devices. You have the voluntary ability to claim credit for a model by
            assigning your name or user handle to the model. Once the model is shared,
            your claimed credit can not be removed from the computers of other users
            who subsequently downloaded the models.
        </p>
<p>
            In addition to your model and profile information, 3D Warehouse collects
            usage information, such as user activity, for example content likes, view
            and downloads, performance metrics data, and log information, which
            includes IP addresses, and browser type.
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            We use your account to associate 3D models to you. You choose to provide
            the information that you want. You can also choose to keep your information
            private and only viewable by you. Your account allows you to interact with
            the 3D Warehouse community, comment, share and collect work, if you choose
            to do so.
        </p>
<p>
            We also track anonymous usage metrics to understand product usage and
            improve product performance.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You have direct control of your personal information via the 3D Warehouse
            profile. To access it, log onto the <a href="https://3dwarehouse.sketchup.com/?login=true">3D Warehouse</a> and
            click on the profile icon in the top right corner of the web page. To
            delete your account, please use the <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com">delete your data form</a>.
        </p>
<p>
            You can find supplemental product specific terms in the <a href="https://3dwarehouse.sketchup.com/tos.html"> SketchUp 3D Warehouse terms of use</a>.
        </p>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp Extension Warehouse
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            The <a href="https://extensions.sketchup.com">Extension Warehouse</a>
            allows you to upload, download and purchase SketchUp extensions. There are
            two types of users of the Extension Warehouse, those that download
            extensions, and those that develop extensions. Users are required to login
            to download or develop extensions. The Extension Warehouse relies on
            Trimble ID for authentication. You can choose to add profile information,
            such as a bio and photo, or not. You have the ability to opt-in to
            notifications through your profile. Your profile information is stored
            within the Extension Warehouse website and is only shared with extension
            developers if you require support for one of their extensions.
        </p>
<p>
            SketchUp collects additional information from extension developers. The
            extension developer
            <a href="http://extensions.sketchup.com/developer-terms-of-service">
                terms of service
            </a>
            can be found online. Extension developers can make extensions available for
            free through the Extension Warehouse, sell their extensions through the
            Extension Warehouse, or make the extension available on the Extension
            Warehouse, but collect payment through their website.
        </p>
<p>
            The Extension Warehouse collects usage information, such as user activity,
            performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses,
            browser type, and error and crash information.
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            If you purchase extensions through the Extension Warehouse, we will collect
            billing information necessary to process an order. We use your account to
            associate extensions to you. You choose to provide the information that you
            want. You can also choose to keep your information private. Your profile
            allows you to interact with the Extension Warehouse community, comment,
            share and collect work, if you choose to do so.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You have direct control of your personal information via the Extension
            Warehouse profile. To access it, log onto the <a href="https://extensions.sketchup.com">Extension Warehouse</a> and click
            on the profile icon in the top right corner of the web page. To delete your
            account, please use the <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com">delete your data form</a> .
        </p>
<p>
            You can find supplemental product specific terms in the <a href="https://extensions.sketchup.com/en/legal"> SketchUp Extension Warehouse terms of use</a>.
        </p>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp.com
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            The SketchUp.com website provides information on SketchUp-related products
            and links you to other SketchUp services. On the SketchUp website, you can
            opt-in to newsletters which include marketing materials and tips on how to
            use SketchUp products. If you download a SketchUp trial, you will be asked
            to provide some basic information such as first name, last name, email
            address, company, country and province where you work. You can opt-out of
            marketing emails when you provide your information. If you are outside of
            the United States, you can ask to have your information forwarded to a
            local reseller that can help you with SketchUp products. SketchUp.com uses
            web browser cookies to remember information about your visit, like your
            preferred language and your page view history.
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            Information gathered during SketchUp trials is used to provide you
            information regarding SketchUp products. If you are a user outside the of
            United States, and you requested to have a local reseller contact you, we
            will share your name, email address and company information with the
            reseller.
        </p>
<p>
            The cookie information we collect can make our site and products more
            useful to you. We also use this information to serve you ads relevant to
            SketchUp on other websites and social networks.
        </p>
<p>
            The SketchUp website also collects usage information, such as user
            activity, performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP
            addresses, browser type, and error and crash information.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You can opt-out of marketing email by clicking on the unsubscribe link included in all SketchUp marketing emails. You can also visit the <a href="https://get.sketchup.com/unsubscribe.html">unsubscribe page</a>. If you wish to delete account, product or support information, please use the <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com"> delete your data form</a>. You can opt out of ads we show you by interacting with them directly, or by setting your cookie preferences on SketchUp.com to turn off targeting cookies.
        </p>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            SketchUp Forums
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            The SketchUp Forum is a place to share SketchUp experiences, ask questions,
            and fix problems through ongoing conversation. In order to participate,
            users need to create an account. A profile is created for you when you
            create a SketchUp Forum account and you are able to choose how much
            information you’d like to disclose. You will also have the ability to
            opt-in to notifications through your profile. Your profile information is
            stored within the Forums website and is never shared with third parties.
        </p>
<p>
            The SketchUp Forum website collects usage information, such as user
            activity, performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP
            addresses, browser type, and error and crash information.
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            We use your account to associate your conversations and posts to you. You
            choose to provide the information that you want to share. You can also
            choose to keep your information private. Your profile allows you to
            interact with members of the SketchUp community and comment, if you choose
            to do so.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            You have direct control of your personal information via the SketchUp Forum
            profile. To access it, log onto the <a href="https://forums.sketchup.com/">SketchUp Community Forum</a> and
            click on the profile icon in the top right corner of the web page. You can
            delete your account directly from your account preferences page.
        </p>

            contact you.

            support request will be tracked to completion in out support system.
        </p>

            The Help Center website collects usage information, such as user activity,
            performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses,
            browser type, and error and crash information.
        </p>
<h4>

        </p>

<h3>
            Sefaira Website
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            The Sefaira.com website provides information related to Sefaira products
            and allows you to opt-in to newsletters which include marketing materials
            and tips on how to use Sefaira products. If you request a Sefaira trial,
            you will be asked to provide some basic information such as first name,
            last name, email address, profession, company, and country where you work.
        </p>
<p>
            Sefaira uses cookies to remember information about your visit, like pages
            visited. That allows us to understand usage of our website and whether
            users can readily find important information.
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            Information gathered during the Sefaira trial request is used to create a
            30-day Sefaira application account. If you opted-in to marketing emails,
            information regarding offers and tips on using Sefaira products will be
            sent to your email address.
        </p>
<p>
            Cookie information is used for many purposes. They are used, for example,
            to remember preferences, to count visitors to a page, or to help you sign
            up for Sefaira services.
        </p>
<p>
            The Sefaira website collects usage information, such as user activity,
            performance metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses,
            browser type, and error and crash information.

        </h4>

            included in all Sefaira marketing emails. You can also visit the <a href="http://sefaira.com/manage-subscriptions/">subscription management page</a>. If you wish to delete account, product or support information, please use
            the <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com">delete your data form</a>.
        </p>
<p>
            You can find supplemental product specific terms in the <a href="http://sefaira.com/msa/">Sefaira Terms of Service</a>.
        </p>

<div class="page-section">
<h3>
            Sefaira Applications
        </h3>
<h4>
            What we collect
        </h4>
<p>
            The Sefaira web application is the website that runs the performance
            analysis of your model. Users are required to login in order to use the
            application. A user profile is created for you when you are added to a
            Sefaira account as a trial user and/or by your account administrator. We
            capture basic information about you such as your first name, last name,
            email, and password. You have the ability to opt-in to notifications
            through your profile. Your profile information is stored within the Sefaira
            application and is never shared with third parties.
        </p>
<p>
            In addition to your profile information, Sefaira collects usage
            information, such as projects you own or have access to, user events (e.g.
            the uploading of models, number of analysis run by users, performance
            metrics data, and log information, which includes IP addresses, and browser
            type).
        </p>
<h4>
            How we use that information
        </h4>
<p>
            The information allows us to understand the usage of the product, and helps
            to guide the development of new functionality. It also enables us to help
            you use the product better. Your profile information is never shared with
            third parties.
        </p>
<h4>
            How to access, update, and protect information
        </h4>
<p>
            If you wish to delete your Sefaira account, please use the <a href="https://privacy.sketchup.com">delete your data form</a>.
        </p>
